\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Klenke 5.11: Markov inequality. Compare with \isa{{\isasymlbrakk}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isasymlambda}x{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}u\ x\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ indicator\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}A\ x{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymin}\ borel{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}measurable\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}M{\isacharsemicolon}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}A\ {\isasymin}\ sets\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}M{\isasymrbrakk}\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ emeasure\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}M\ {\isacharbraceleft}{\kern0pt}x\ {\isasymin}\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}A{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ {\isadigit{1}}\ {\isasymle}\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}c\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}u\ x{\isacharbraceright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymle}\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}c\ {\isacharasterisk}{\kern0pt}\ set{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}nn{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}integral\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}M\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}A\ {\isacharquery}{\kern0pt}u}%

\ \ \isacommand{qed}\isamarkupfalse%
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
In the textbook, we define the following:
  A_n(\<gamma>) = {x. max {dist (X ((k - 1) * 2 powr - n) x) (X (k * 2 powr - n) x), k \<in> {0..2^n}} \<ge> 2 powr -\<gamma> * n}
  B_n = \<Union>m\<ge>n. A_m
  N = limsup (n -> \<infinity>) A_n = \<Inter>n. B_n
  
  We then go on to prove that N is a null set. N characterises the set of points that are
  not Holder continuous, and we can therefore define our continuous modification on M - N.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\ \ \ \ \ \ \isacommand{qed}\isamarkupfalse%
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
The objective of this block is to show that, for dyadic numbers s t with the same resolution:
     | X t \<omega> - x s \<omega> | \<le> 2 * 2 powr (- \<gamma> * n) / (1 - 2 powr - \<gamma>)
    Holder continuity on dyadic numbers follows directly from this fact.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Because the processes are indistinguishable, they are all equal on \<omega>, so the local holder
  continuity extends to {0..}.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
